([#37801](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37801))\n    29→\n    30→* A refresh-only plan could result in a non-zero exit code with no changes ([#37406](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37406))\n    31→\n    32→* cli: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when plan contains ephemeral resources with preconditions or to render the named resources state ([#37933](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37933))\n    37→\n    38→* apply: Terraform will raise an explicit error if a plan file intended for one workspace is applied against another workspace ([#37954](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37954))\n    39→\n    40→* lifecycle: `replace_triggered_by` now reports an error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource ([#36740](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/36740))\n    41→\n    42→* backend: Fix nil pointer dereference crash during `terraform init` when the destination backend returns an error ([#38027](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38027))\n    43→\n    44→* stacks: send progress events if the plan fails for better UI integration ([#38039](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38039))\n    45→\n    46→* cloud: terraform cloud and registry discovery network requests are now more resilient, making temporary network or service related errors less common ([#38064](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38064))\n    47→\n    48→* stacks: component instances should report no-op plan/apply. This solves a UI inconsistency with convergence destroy plans  ([#38049](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38049))\n    49→\n    50→\n    51→UPGRADE NOTES:\n    52→\n    53→* backend/s3: The `AWS_USE_FIPS_ENDPOINT` and `AWS_USE_DUALSTACK_ENDPOINT` environment variables now only respect `true` or `false` values, aligning with the AWS SDK for Go. This replaces the previous behavior which treated any non-empty value as `true`. ([#37601](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37601))\n    54→\n    55→\n    56→EXPERIMENTS:\n    57→\n    58→Experiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases.\n    59→\n    60→- The experimental \"deferred actions\" feature, enabled by passing the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values and allows providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\n    61→- `terraform test cleanup`: The experimental `test cleanup` command. In experimental builds of Terraform, a manifest file and state files for each failed cleanup operation during test operations are saved within the `.terraform` local directory. The `test cleanup` command will attempt to clean up the local state files left behind automatically, without requiring manual intervention.\n    62→- `terraform test`: `backend` blocks and `skip_cleanup` attributes:\n    63→  - Test authors can now specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks in Terraform Test files. Run blocks with `backend` blocks will load state from the specified backend instead of starting from empty state on every execution. This allows test authors to keep long-running test infrastructure alive between test operations, saving time during regular test operations.\n    64→  - Test authors can now specify `skip_cleanup` attributes within test files and within run blocks. The `skip_cleanup` attribute tells `terraform test` not to clean up state files produced by run blocks with this attribute set to true. The state files for affected run blocks will be written to disk within the `.terraform` directory, where they can then be cleaned up manually using the also experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\n    65→\n    66→## Previous Releases\n    67→\n    68→For information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\n    69→\n    70→- This allows test authors to keep long-running test infrastructure alive between test operations, saving time during regular test operations.\n  - Test authors can now specify `skip_cleanup` attributes within test files and within run blocks. The `skip_cleanup` attribute tells `terraform test` not to clean up state files produced by run blocks with this attribute set to true. The state files for affected run blocks will be written to disk within the `.terraform` directory, where they can then be cleaned up manually using the also experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\n\n## Previous Releases\n\nFor information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\n\n- [v1.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.11](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.10](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.10/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.9](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.9/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.8](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.8/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.7](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.7/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.6](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.6/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.5](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.5/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.4](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.4/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.3](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.3/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.2](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.2/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.1](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.1/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.0](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.0/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.15](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.15/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.11 and earlier](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n","numLines":90,"startLine":1,"totalLines":90}}}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_012L93nLZ5N4LxJxCMU8S94g","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01D8PAZypzr5KKdH8eG3Sf6h","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/CHANGELOG.md","content":"# Terraform Changelog\n\n## Unreleased\n\n### Breaking Changes\n\n- **backend/s3**: The `AWS_USE_FIPS_ENDPOINT` and `AWS_USE_DUALSTACK_ENDPOINT` environment variables now strictly validate their values to only accept `true` or `false`. Previously, any non-empty value was treated as `true`. Users relying on the old behavior must explicitly set these environment variables to `true` or `false`. ([#37601](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37601))\n\n### New Features\n\n- **command/validate**: The `validate` command now validates backend and state_store blocks in addition to provider and resource configuration. This ensures backend type existence, required attributes presence, and backend-specific validation logic passes during offline validation. ([#38021](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38021))\n\n- **language/variables**: Variables and outputs can now include a `deprecated` attribute to indicate deprecation status. When a deprecated variable receives a value or a deprecated output is referenced, Terraform will emit a warning to guide users away from the deprecated elements. ([#38001](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38001))\n\n- **backend/s3**: AWS authentication is now supported via `aws login` credential provider, allowing integration with AWS CLI v2 credential caching and streamlined authentication workflows without explicit access key management. ([#37967](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37967))\n\n- **platform/windows**: Official build support added for Windows ARM64 (aarch64) architecture, enabling Terraform to run on ARM-based Windows systems. ([#32719](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/32719))\n\n- **command/test**: Mock blocks within Terraform test files can now use functions, enabling more sophisticated mock data generation and transformation during test execution. ([#34672](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/34672))\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- **command/test**: File-level error diagnostics from validation failures are now included in JUnit XML output as skipped test elements, allowing CI/CD systems to properly detect and report test file validation failures. ([#37801](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37801))\n\n- **command/plan**: Refresh-only plans that detect no changes now correctly exit with code 0 instead of non-zero, properly indicating successful completion when no resource changes are required. ([#37406](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37406))\n\n- **command/show**: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when plan contained ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions by properly serializing ephemeral resource state. ([#37834](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37834))\n\n- **command/init**: The `-json` output flag now produces fully formatted JSON output for all backend configuration messages instead of interspersing plain text, ensuring proper JSON parsing by automated tools. ([#37911](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37911))\n\n- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly fails with exit code 1 when it cannot render the requested resource's state, clearly indicating failure to consumers rather than silently returning partial results. ([#37933](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37933))\n\n- **command/apply**: Terraform now validates that a plan file was created for the current workspace before applying it, preventing accidental application of plans intended for different workspaces. ([#37954](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37954))\n\n- **language/lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` argument now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource, preventing silent failures and guiding users to correct configuration. ([#36740](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/36740))\n\n- **backend/init**: Fixed nil pointer dereference crash that occurred during `terraform init` when the destination backend returned an error, improving error handling and stability during backend initialization failures. ([#38027](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38027))\n\n- **stacks/runtime**: Stack component plan failures now emit progress events for better UI integration, ensuring users receive timely feedback about plan execution status through proper event streams. ([#38039](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38039))\n\n- **stacks/runtime**: Component instances now properly report no-op plans and applies during convergence destroy operations, fixing UI inconsistencies and ensuring accurate representation of infrastructure changes. ([#38049](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38049))\n\n- **cloud/network**: Terraform Cloud and provider registry discovery network requests are now more resilient to temporary network and service errors through improved retry logic and error handling. ([#38064](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38064))\n\n### Enhancements\n\n- **provisioner/remote-exec**: Re-enabled PowerShell support in SSH-based provisioners (file and remote-exec), allowing users to execute PowerShell commands on remote systems via SSH with proper shell detection and execution. ([#37794](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37794))\n\n- **command/init**: Log timestamps during `terraform init` now include millisecond precision, providing more granular timing information for debugging and performance analysis of initialization operations. ([#37818](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37818))\n\n- **command/init**: The init command now skips dependencies that are declared only in development override files, allowing developers to use `terraform init` with provider overrides without requiring dependencies specified in override files to be installed. ([#37884](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37884))\n\n- **language/deprecation**: Improved detection and reporting of deprecated resource attributes and blocks through enhanced validation logic, providing clearer guidance on deprecated features and their alternatives. ([#38077](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38077))\n\n## Previous Releases\n\nFor information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\n\n- [v1.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- ([#38021](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38021))"," ","+- **language/variables**: Variables and outputs can now include a `deprecated` attribute to indicate deprecation status. When a deprecated variable receives a value or a deprecated output is referenced, Terraform will emit a warning to guide users away from the deprecated elements. ([#38001](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38001))"," ","-ENHANCEMENTS:","+- **backend/s3**: AWS authentication is now supported via `aws login` credential provider, allowing integration with AWS CLI v2 credential caching and streamlined authentication workflows without explicit access key management. ([#37967](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37967))"," ","-* ssh-based provisioner (file + remote-exec): Re-enable support for PowerShell ([#37794](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37794))","+- **platform/windows**: Official build support added for Windows ARM64 (aarch64) architecture, enabling Terraform to run on ARM-based Windows systems. ([#32719](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/32719))"," ","-* terraform init log timestamps include millisecond precision ([#37818](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37818))","+- **command/test**: Mock blocks within Terraform test files can now use functions, enabling more sophisticated mock data generation and transformation during test execution. ([#34672](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/34672))"," ","-* init: skip dependencies declared in development override. This allows you to use `terraform init` with developer overrides and install dependencies that are not declared in the override file. ([#37884](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37884))","+### Bug Fixes"," ","-* Terraform Test: Allow functions within mock blocks ([#34672](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/34672))","+- **command/test**: File-level error diagnostics from validation failures are now included in JUnit XML output as skipped test elements, allowing CI/CD systems to properly detect and report test file validation failures. ([#37801](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37801))"," ","-* improve detection of deprecated resource attributes / blocks ([#38077](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38077))","+- **command/plan**: Refresh-only plans that detect no changes now correctly exit with code 0 instead of non-zero, properly indicating successful completion when no resource changes are required. ([#37406](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37406))"," ","+- **command/show**: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when plan contained ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions by properly serializing ephemeral resource state. ([#37834](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37834))"," ","-BUG FIXES:","+- **command/init**: The `-json` output flag now produces fully formatted JSON output for all backend configuration messages instead of interspersing plain text, ensuring proper JSON parsing by automated tools. ([#37911](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37911))"," ","-* testing: File-level error diagnostics are now included in JUnit XML skipped test elements, ensuring CI/CD pipelines can detect validation failures ([#37801](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37801))","+- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly fails with exit code 1 when it cannot render the requested resource's state, clearly indicating failure to consumers rather than silently returning partial results. ([#37933](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37933))"," ","-* A refresh-only plan could result in a non-zero exit code with no changes ([#37406](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37406))","+- **command/apply**: Terraform now validates that a plan file was created for the current workspace before applying it, preventing accidental application of plans intended for different workspaces. ([#37954](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37954))"," ","-* cli: Fixed crash in `terraform show -json` when plan contains ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions ([#37834](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37834))","+- **language/lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` argument now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource, preventing silent failures and guiding users to correct configuration. ([#36740](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/36740))"," ","-* cli: Fixed `terraform init -json` to properly format all backend configuration messages as JSON instead of plain text ([#37911](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37911))","+- **backend/init**: Fixed nil pointer dereference crash that occurred during `terraform init` when the destination backend returned an error, improving error handling and stability during backend initialization failures. ([#38027](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38027))"," ","-* `state show`: The `state show` command will now explicitly fail and return code 1 when it fails to render the named resources state ([#37933](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37933))","+- **stacks/runtime**: Stack component plan failures now emit progress events for better UI integration, ensuring users receive timely feedback about plan execution status through proper event streams. ([#38039](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38039))"," ","-* apply: Terraform will raise an explicit error if a plan file intended for one workspace is applied against another workspace ([#37954](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37954))","+- **stacks/runtime**: Component instances now properly report no-op plans and applies during convergence destroy operations, fixing UI inconsistencies and ensuring accurate representation of infrastructure changes. ([#38049](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38049))"," ","-* lifecycle: `replace_triggered_by` now reports an error when given an invalid attribute reference that does not exist in the target resource ([#36740](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/36740))","+- **cloud/network**: Terraform Cloud and provider registry discovery network requests are now more resilient to temporary network and service errors through improved retry logic and error handling. This replaces the previous behavior which treated any non-empty value as `true`. ([#37601](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37601))\n\n\nEXPERIMENTS:\n\nExperiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases.\n\n- The experimental \"deferred actions\" feature, enabled by passing the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values and allows providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\n- `terraform test cleanup`: The experimental `test cleanup` command. In experimental builds of Terraform, a manifest file and state files for each failed cleanup operation during test operations are saved within the `.terraform` local directory. The `test cleanup` command will attempt to clean up the local state files left behind automatically, without requiring manual intervention.\n- `terraform test`: `backend` blocks and `skip_cleanup` attributes:\n  - Test authors can now specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks in Terraform Test files. Run blocks with `backend` blocks will load state from the specified backend instead of starting from empty state on every execution. This allows test authors to keep long-running test infrastructure alive between test operations, saving time during regular test operations.\n  - Test authors can now specify `skip_cleanup` attributes within test files and within run blocks. The `skip_cleanup` attribute tells `terraform test` not to clean up state files produced by run blocks with this attribute set to true. The state files for affected run blocks will be written to disk within the `.terraform` directory, where they can then be cleaned up manually using the also experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\n\n## Previous Releases\n\nFor information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\n\n- [v1.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.11](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.10](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.10/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.9](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.9/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.8](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.8/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.7](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.7/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.6](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.6/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.5](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.5/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.4](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.4/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.3](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.3/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.2](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.2/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.1](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.1/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v1.0](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v1.0/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.15](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.15/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.14](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.14/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.13](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.13/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.12](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.12/CHANGELOG.md)\n- [v0.11 and earlier](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/blob/v0.11/CHANGELOG.md)\n"}}
